    product_name TEXT,
    price DECIMAL,
    category TEXT
);

    order_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id INT,
    order_date DATE,
    total_amount DECIMAL
);

    customer_name TEXT,
    email TEXT,
    address TEXT
);

    order_item_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    order_id INT,
    product_id INT,
    quantity INT,
    total_price DECIMAL
);

);

    order_date DATE
);

    customer_name STRING,
    email STRING,
    address STRING
);

    order_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id UUID,
    product_id UUID,
    quantity INT,
    order_date DATE
);

    product_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    product_name STRING,
    price DECIMAL,
    category STRING
);

);
